    		const storedTheme =

    		const theme =
    			storedTheme ||
    			(window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: light)').matches ? 'light' : 'dark');

    					const tmpl = document.querySelector(`#theme-icons`);
    					const newIcon = tmpl && tmpl.content.querySelector('.' + theme);

    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="windows-recommended">Windows (Recommended)</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#windows-recommended"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Windows (Recommended)”</span></a></div>
    <ol>
    <li>
    <p>Download the repository as a ZIP from the <a href="https://github.com/alan7383/playify">GitHub releases</a> or clone it via git.</p>
    <p><img alt="Download ZIP" loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="983" height="433" src="/_astro/download-zip.DHv4izbq_1eBVFP.webp" srcset=""></p>
    </li>
    <li>
    <p>Extract the ZIP file anywhere on your computer (make sure it’s extracted, do not run from within the ZIP).</p>
    </li>
    <li>
    <p>Double-click <code dir="auto">start.bat</code>.</p>
    </li>
    <li>
    <p>The Playify installer will automatically install Python, download FFmpeg, and prompt you for your Discord Token and Spotify keys.</p>
    </li>
    <li>
    <p>The TUI Dashboard will launch automatically!</p>
    </li>
    </ol>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="linux">Linux</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#linux"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Linux”</span></a></div>
    <p>Playify natively supports Linux with an automated setup script.</p>
    <ol>
    <li>Clone the repository:</li>
    </ol>
    <div class="expressive-code"><link rel="stylesheet" href="/_astro/ec.v4551.css"><script type="module" src="/_astro/ec.0vx5m.js"></script><figure class="frame is-terminal not-content"><figcaption class="header"><span class="title"></span><span class="sr-only">Terminal window</span></figcaption><pre data-language="bash"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#82AAFF;--1:#3B61B0">git</span><span style="--0:#D6DEEB;--1:#403F53"> </span><span style="--0:#ECC48D;--1:#3B61B0">clone</span><span style="--0:#D6DEEB;--1:#403F53"> </span><span style="--0:#ECC48D;--1:#3B61B0">https://github.com/alan7383/playify.git</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="git clone https://github.com/alan7383/playify.git"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
    <ol start="2">
    <li>Enter the directory:</li>
    </ol>
    <div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame is-terminal not-content"><figcaption class="header"><span class="title"></span><span class="sr-only">Terminal window</span></figcaption><pre data-language="bash"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#C5E478;--1:#3B61B0">cd</span><span style="--0:#D6DEEB;--1:#403F53"> </span><span style="--0:#ECC48D;--1:#3B61B0">playify</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="cd playify"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
    <ol start="3">
    <li>Run the bootstrapper:</li>
    </ol>
    <div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame is-terminal not-content"><figcaption class="header"><span class="title"></span><span class="sr-only">Terminal window</span></figcaption><pre data-language="bash"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#82AAFF;--1:#3B61B0">bash</span><span style="--0:#D6DEEB;--1:#403F53"> </span><span style="--0:#ECC48D;--1:#3B61B0">start.sh</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="bash start.sh"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
    <ol start="4">
    <li>The script will set up your virtual environment, automatically download a local copy of FFmpeg, and launch the Dashboard.</li>
    </ol>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="docker">Docker</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#docker"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Docker”</span></a></div>
    <p>If you prefer using Docker:</p>

astro-67yu43on">  <main data-pagefind-body class="astro-bguv2lll" lang="en" dir="ltr">    <div class="content-panel astro-7nkwcw3z"> <div class="sl-container astro-7nkwcw3z"> <h1 id="_top" class="astro-j6tvhyss">Introduction</h1> </div> </div> <div class="content-panel astro-7nkwcw3z"> <div class="sl-container astro-7nkwcw3z"> <div class="sl-markdown-content"> <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h1"><h1 id="playify">Playify</h1><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#playify"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Playify”</span></a></div>
    <p><strong>Playify</strong> is an open-source Discord music bot built for simplicity. No web UI, no paywalls, no account required — just slash commands and music.</p>
    <p>Playify has been completely rewritten in V2 to provide a seamless, robust, and beautiful experience directly from your terminal.</p>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="key-features">Key Features</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#key-features"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Key Features”</span></a></div>
    <ul>
    <li><strong>Interactive TUI dashboard</strong>: Monitor resources, queue length, active players, and logs in real-time through a beautiful ASCII interface.</li>
    <li><strong>Built-in auto-updater</strong>: Keep your bot up to date directly from the dashboard. No <code dir="auto">git pull</code> or manual downloads required.</li>
    <li><strong>One-click installer</strong>: Run the setup script and let Playify automatically install Python, download FFmpeg, and set up your <code dir="auto">.env</code> configuration.</li>
    <li><strong>In-app settings menu</strong>: Configure your bot’s Discord presence, default volumes, and UI customization without touching a text file.</li>
    </ul>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="sources--playback">Sources &#x26; Playback</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#sources--playback"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Sources &#x26; Playback”</span></a></div>
    <ul>
    <li>Play from <strong>10+ sources</strong>: YouTube, SoundCloud, Twitch, Spotify, Apple Music, etc.</li>
    <li><strong>Direct audio links</strong>: stream any public MP3, FLAC, WAV, or audio URL.</li>
    <li><strong>Local file playback</strong>: upload and play your own audio/video files directly.</li>
    <li><strong>Autoplay</strong> of similar tracks via YouTube Mix and SoundCloud Stations.</li>
    <li><strong>Loop</strong> and <strong>shuffle</strong> queue controls.</li>
    <li>Audio <strong>filters</strong>: slowed, reverb, bass boost, nightcore, and more.</li>
    </ul>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="extras">Extras</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#extras"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Extras”</span></a></div>
    <ul>
    <li><strong>Lyrics</strong> fetching and display for the current track.</li>
    <li><strong>Karaoke mode</strong> with synced lyrics.</li>
    <li><strong>24/7 mode</strong> to keep the bot in a channel permanently.</li>
    <li><strong>Kawaii Mode</strong> — toggle cute kaomoji responses with <code dir="auto">/kaomoji</code>.</li>
    <li><strong>Interactive queue pages</strong>, track removal menus, and a seek interface.</li>
    </ul> </div> <footer class="sl-flex astro-3yyafb3n"> <div class="meta sl-flex astro-3yyafb3n">   </div> <div class="pagination-links print:hidden astro-u2l5gyhi" dir="ltr">  <a href="/getting-started/installation/" rel="next" class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> <svg aria-hidden="true" class="astro-u2l5gyhi astro-c6vsoqas" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" style="--sl-icon-size: 1.5rem;"><path d="M17.92 11.62a1.001 1.001 0 0 0-.21-.33l-5-5a1.003 1.003 0 1 0-1.42 1.42l3.3 3.29H7a1 1 0 0 0 0 2h7.59l-3.3 3.29a1.002 1.002 0 0 0 .325 1.639 1 1 0 0 0 1.095-.219l5-5a1 1 0 0 0 .21-.33 1 1 0 0 0 0-.76Z"/></svg> <span class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> Next <br class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> <span class="link-title astro-u2l5gyhi">Installation</span> </span> </a> </div>  </footer> </div> </div>  </main> </div> </div> </div> </div> </body></html>

Invite to your Server</span> </a>  </li> </ul></nav></starlight-toc><script type="module" src="/_astro/TableOfContents.astro_astro_type_script_index_0_lang.FuRcXuRY.js"></script></div></div> </div> </aside> <div class="main-pane astro-67yu43on">  <main data-pagefind-body class="astro-bguv2lll" lang="en" dir="ltr">    <div class="content-panel astro-7nkwcw3z"> <div class="sl-container astro-7nkwcw3z"> <h1 id="_top" class="astro-j6tvhyss">Inviting the Bot</h1> </div> </div> <div class="content-panel astro-7nkwcw3z"> <div class="sl-container astro-7nkwcw3z"> <div class="sl-markdown-content"> <p>Once you have your bot running (or if you are setting up the bot application for the first time), you need to invite the bot to your Discord server! It does not join automatically.</p>
    <p>Follow these steps to generate an invite link for your bot.</p>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="1-go-to-the-developer-portal">1. Go to the Developer Portal</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#1-go-to-the-developer-portal"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “1. Go to the Developer Portal”</span></a></div>
    <p>Go to the <a href="https://discord.com/developers/applications">Discord Developer Portal</a> and select your application. If you don’t have one yet, you must create one by clicking <strong>New Application</strong>.</p>
    <p><img alt="New Application" loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1317" height="517" src="/_astro/new-application.Bq6hjQ5v_2oVj9g.webp" srcset=""></p>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="2-open-the-url-generator">2. Open the URL Generator</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#2-open-the-url-generator"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “2. Open the URL Generator”</span></a></div>
    <p>In the sidebar on the left, click on <strong>OAuth2</strong>, and then select <strong>URL Generator</strong>.</p>
    <p><img alt="OAuth2 Menu" loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="251" height="639" src="/_astro/oauth2.DLh1MJ7s_12Oa6T.webp" srcset=""></p>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="3-select-scopes-and-permissions">3. Select Scopes and Permissions</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#3-select-scopes-and-permissions"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “3. Select Scopes and Permissions”</span></a></div>
    <p>To ensure Playify functions correctly and can register its slash commands, you must select the correct scopes and permissions.</p>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h3"><h3 id="scopes">Scopes</h3><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#scopes"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Scopes”</span></a></div>
    <p>Check the following boxes:</p>
    <ul>
    <li><code dir="auto">bot</code></li>
    <li><code dir="auto">applications.commands</code></li>
    </ul>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h3"><h3 id="bot-permissions">Bot Permissions</h3><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#bot-permissions"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Bot Permissions”</span></a></div>
    <p>Once you check <code dir="auto">bot</code>, a list of permissions will appear below. Check the following:</p>
    <ul>
    <li><code dir="auto">View Channels</code></li>
    <li><code dir="auto">Send Messages</code></li>
    <li><code dir="auto">Embed Links</code></li>
    <li><code dir="auto">Read Message History</code></li>
    <li><code dir="auto">Connect</code></li>
    <li><code dir="auto">Speak</code></li>
    </ul>
    <p><em>(Alternatively, if you trust your own bot and don’t want to deal with specific permissions, you can simply check <code dir="auto">Administrator</code>.)</em></p>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="4-generate-and-open-the-url">4. Generate and Open the URL</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#4-generate-and-open-the-url"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “4. Generate and Open the URL”</span></a></div>
    <p>At the bottom of the page, a Generated URL will appear. Copy this URL and open it in a new tab in your web browser.</p>
    <p><img alt="Generated URL" loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1416" height="300" src="/_astro/generated-url.GVBdvuc4_Z1LLKA2.webp" srcset=""></p>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="5-invite-to-your-server">5. Invite to your Server</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#5-invite-to-your-server"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “5. Invite to your Server”</span></a></div>
    <p>Select the server you want to add Playify to, and confirm.</p>
    <p>Once it’s in, join a Voice Channel and use <code dir="auto">/play</code> to start listening!</p> </div> <footer class="sl-flex astro-3yyafb3n"> <div class="meta sl-flex astro-3yyafb3n">   </div> <div class="pagination-links print:hidden astro-u2l5gyhi" dir="ltr"> <a href="/getting-started/installation/" rel="prev" class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> <svg aria-hidden="true" class="astro-u2l5gyhi astro-c6vsoqas" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" style="--sl-icon-size: 1.5rem;"><path d="M17 11H9.41l3.3-3.29a1.004 1.004 0 1 0-1.42-1.42l-5 5a1 1 0 0 0-.21.33 1 1 0 0 0 0 .76 1 1 0 0 0 .21.33l5 5a1.002 1.002 0 0 0 1.639-.325 1 1 0 0 0-.219-1.095L9.41 13H17a1 1 0 0 0 0-2Z"/></svg> <span class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> Previous <br class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> <span class="link-title astro-u2l5gyhi">Installation</span> </span> </a> <a href="/usage/commands/" rel="next" class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> <svg aria-hidden="true" class="astro-u2l5gyhi astro-c6vsoqas" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" style="--sl-icon-size: 1.5rem;"><path d="M17.92 11.62a1.001 1.001 0 0 0-.21-.33l-5-5a1.003 1.003 0 1 0-1.42 1.42l3.3 3.29H7a1 1 0 0 0 0 2h7.59l-3.3 3.29a1.002 1.002 0 0 0 .325 1.639 1 1 0 0 0 1.095-.219l5-5a1 1 0 0 0 .21-.33 1 1 0 0 0 0-.76Z"/></svg> <span class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> Next <br class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> <span class="link-title astro-u2l5gyhi">Commands Reference</span> </span> </a> </div>  </footer> </div> </div>  </main> </div> </div> </div> </div> </body></html>

Merged index (${this.basePath}): ${entry_json.version}`,"If you encounter any search errors, make sure that both sites are running the same version of Pagefind."].join("\n"));}}}catch(e){console.error(`Failed to load Pagefind metadata:
    ${e?.toString()}`);throw new Error("Failed to load Pagefind metadata");}}findIndex(language){if(this.languages){let index=this.languages[language];if(index)return index;index=this.languages[language.split("-")[0]];if(index)return index;let topLang=Object.values(this.languages).sort((a,b)=>b.page_count-a.page_count);if(topLang[0])return topLang[0];}throw new Error("Pagefind Error: No language indexes found.");}async loadMeta(index){try{let compressed_resp=await this.throttledFetch(`${this.basePath}pagefind.${index}.pf_meta`);let compressed_meta=await compressed_resp.arrayBuffer();this.searchMeta=this.decompress(new Uint8Array(compressed_meta),"Pagefind metadata");}catch(e){console.error(`Failed to load the meta index:

FICHIER : dist\pagefind\pagefind-component-ui.css

    /*
     * Why all the :is(*, #\#) prefixes?
     *
     * These components are embedded in who-knows-what sites with unpredictable CSS.
     * We need our styles to win against host page selectors like `.content p` or
     * `article a:hover` without using !important everywhere.
     *
     * The :is(*, #\#) trick adds ID-level specificity (0,1,0) without requiring
     * an actual ID in the DOM. Chaining it (2x or 3x) builds enough specificity
     * to beat most host selectors.
     *
     * The #\# is an escaped # character, creating an invalid-but-harmless ID
     * selector that never matches, but still contributes specificity via :is().
     *
     * We also need these overrides to only affect the Component UI elements themselves.
     * Users can provide custom templates to the results and searchbox components,
     * and these must inherit their styles without having to fight ours.
     *
     * It's admittedly a bit of a hack but it does provide best effort styling consistency
     * for the Component UI out in the wild.
     */
    
    :root {
        --pf-text: #1a1a1a;
        --pf-text-secondary: #666;
        --pf-text-muted: #767676;
        --pf-background: #fff;
        --pf-border: #e0e0e0;
        --pf-border-focus: #999;
        --pf-skeleton: #eee;
        --pf-skeleton-shine: #f5f5f5;
        --pf-hover: #f5f5f5;
        --pf-mark: #1a1a1a;
        --pf-scroll-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08);
    
        --pf-shadow-sm: 0 2px 8px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06);
        --pf-shadow-md: 0 4px 12px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1);
        --pf-shadow-lg: 0 16px 48px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
    
        --pf-error-bg: #fef2f2;
        --pf-error-border: #fecaca;
        --pf-error-text: #dc2626;
        --pf-error-text-secondary: #b91c1c;
    
        --pf-outline-focus: #0969da;
        --pf-outline-width: 2px;
        --pf-outline-offset: 2px;
    
        --pf-font:
            -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Segoe UI", Roboto, Helvetica, Arial,
            sans-serif;
    
        --pf-input-height: 36px;
        --pf-input-font-size: 16px;
        --pf-summary-font-size: 12px;
        --pf-result-title-font-size: 14px;
        --pf-result-excerpt-font-size: 13px;
        --pf-modal-backdrop: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.5);
        --pf-results-display: flex;
        --pf-results-flex-direction: column;
        --pf-results-flex-wrap: nowrap;
        --pf-results-columns: none;
        --pf-results-gap: 8px;

        return urlParams.getAll(paramName);
      }
      // Inline styles might be too hard to override
      addHighlightStyles(className) {
        if (!className) return;
        const styleElement = document.createElement("style");
        styleElement.innerText = `:where(.${className}) { background-color: yellow; color: black; }`;
        document.head.appendChild(styleElement);
      }

        if (this.markContext) {
          return new import_mark.default(this.markContext);
        }
        const pagefindBody = document.querySelectorAll("[data-pagefind-body]");
        if (pagefindBody.length !== 0) {
          return new import_mark.default(pagefindBody);
        } else {
          return new import_mark.default(document.body);
        }
      }
      markText(instance, text) {
        instance.mark(text, this.markOptions);
      }

        const params = this.getHighlightParams(this.highlightParam);
        if (!params || params.length === 0) return;

asyncSleep(50);}await newInstance.init(options.language||this.primaryLanguage,{load_wasm:false});const{language,...remainingOptions}=options;await newInstance.options(remainingOptions);}mergeFilters(filters){const merged={};for(const searchFilter of filters){for(const[filterKey,values]of Object.entries(searchFilter)){if(!merged[filterKey]){merged[filterKey]=values;continue;}else{const filter=merged[filterKey];for(const[valueKey,count]of Object.entries(values)){filter[valueKey]=(filter[valueKey]||0)+count;}}}}return merged;}async filters(){let filters=await Promise.all(this.instances.map((i2)=>i2.filters()));return this.search(term,options);if(thisSearchID!==this.searchID){return null;}return searchResult;}async search(term,options={}){let search=await results=search.map((s)=>s.results).flat().sort((a,b)=>b.score-a.score);const timings=search.map((s)=>s.timings);const unfilteredResultCount=search.reduce((sum,s)=>sum+s.unfilteredResultCount,0);let response={results,unfilteredResultCount,filters,totalFilters,timings};if(search[0].search_keywords){response.search_keywords=search[0].search_keywords;}if(search[0].query_term_idfs){response.query_term_idfs=search[0].query_term_idfs;}return response;}};var dataCallbacks=new Map();var instanceDataIds=new Map();var instances=new Map();var DEFAULT_INSTANCE="default";var getInstance=(instanceId)=>{const instance=instances.get(instanceId);if(!instance){throw new Error(`Pagefind instance "${instanceId}" not initialized`);}return instance;};var pagefindInstance=getInstance(instanceId);const[term,options]=args;await pagefindInstance.preload(term,options);return{id,result:true};}case"filters":{const pagefindInstance=getInstance(instanceId);const result=await pagefindInstance.filters();return{id,result};}case"getData":{const[dataId]=args;const callback=dataCallbacks.get(dataId);if(!callback?.getData){return{id,result:null};}const data=await callback.getData();return{id,result:data};}case"releaseData":{const[dataId]=args;dataCallbacks.delete(dataId);instanceDataIds.get(instanceId)?.delete(dataId);return{id,result:true};}case"destroy":{instances.delete(instanceId);const astro-67yu43on">  <main data-pagefind-body class="astro-bguv2lll" lang="en" dir="ltr">    <div class="content-panel astro-7nkwcw3z"> <div class="sl-container astro-7nkwcw3z"> <h1 id="_top" class="astro-j6tvhyss">FAQ &amp; Troubleshooting</h1> </div> </div> <div class="content-panel astro-7nkwcw3z"> <div class="sl-container astro-7nkwcw3z"> <div class="sl-markdown-content"> <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="the-bot-says-ffmpeg-is-not-found-when-trying-to-play-music">The bot says “FFmpeg is not found” when trying to play music!</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#the-bot-says-ffmpeg-is-not-found-when-trying-to-play-music"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “The bot says “FFmpeg is not found” when trying to play music!”</span></a></div>
    <p>Playify normally downloads FFmpeg automatically. If it failed:</p>
    <ol>
    <li>You can manually download <code dir="auto">ffmpeg.exe</code> and place it in the <code dir="auto">bin/</code> folder inside your Playify directory (create the <code dir="auto">bin</code> folder if it doesn’t exist).</li>
    <li><a href="https://www.videohelp.com/download/ffmpeg-6.1.1-full_build.7z?r=zndlFgBq">Download FFmpeg 6.1.1 here</a> (extract and grab <code dir="auto">ffmpeg.exe</code> from the <code dir="auto">bin</code> folder).</li>
    </ol>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="do-i-need-to-enter-my-tokens-every-time">Do I need to enter my tokens every time?</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#do-i-need-to-enter-my-tokens-every-time"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Do I need to enter my tokens every time?”</span></a></div>
    <p>Nope! The setup script saves your tokens in a <code dir="auto">.env</code> file. The next time you want to start the bot, just double-click <code dir="auto">start.bat</code> (or run <code dir="auto">start.sh</code>). It will instantly start the bot without asking for tokens again.</p>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="spotify-errors-or-tracks-not-loading">Spotify errors or tracks not loading</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#spotify-errors-or-tracks-not-loading"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Spotify errors or tracks not loading”</span></a></div>
    <p>Check your <code dir="auto">SPOTIFY_CLIENT_ID</code> and <code dir="auto">SPOTIFY_CLIENT_SECRET</code> in your <code dir="auto">.env</code> file. You can get these by creating an app in the <a href="https://developer.spotify.com/dashboard/">Spotify Developer Dashboard</a>.</p>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="bot-is-offline-or-unresponsive">Bot is offline or unresponsive</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#bot-is-offline-or-unresponsive"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Bot is offline or unresponsive”</span></a></div>
    <ul>
    <li>Verify your <code dir="auto">DISCORD_TOKEN</code> in the <code dir="auto">.env</code> file.</li>
    <li>Ensure you have invited the bot with the correct scopes and permissions (<code dir="auto">bot</code>, <code dir="auto">applications.commands</code>). See the <a href="/getting-started/inviting-the-bot">Inviting the Bot</a> guide for details.</li>
    </ul> </div> <footer class="sl-flex astro-3yyafb3n"> <div class="meta sl-flex astro-3yyafb3n">   </div> <div class="pagination-links print:hidden astro-u2l5gyhi" dir="ltr"> <a href="/usage/tui-dashboard/" rel="prev" class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> <svg aria-hidden="true" class="astro-u2l5gyhi astro-c6vsoqas" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" style="--sl-icon-size: 1.5rem;"><path d="M17 11H9.41l3.3-3.29a1.004 1.004 0 1 0-1.42-1.42l-5 5a1 1 0 0 0-.21.33 1 1 0 0 0 0 .76 1 1 0 0 0 .21.33l5 5a1.002 1.002 0 0 0 1.639-.325 1 1 0 0 0-.219-1.095L9.41 13H17a1 1 0 0 0 0-2Z"/></svg> <span class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> Previous <br class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> <span class="link-title astro-u2l5gyhi">TUI Dashboard</span> </span> </a>  </div>  </footer> </div> </div>  </main> </div> </div> </div> </div> </body></html>

    	window.StarlightThemeProvider = (() => {
    		const storedTheme =
    			typeof localStorage !== 'undefined' && localStorage.getItem('starlight-theme');
    		const theme =
    			storedTheme ||
    			(window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: light)').matches ? 'light' : 'dark');
    		document.documentElement.dataset.theme = theme === 'light' ? 'light' : 'dark';
    		return {
    			updatePickers(theme = storedTheme || 'auto') {
    				document.querySelectorAll('starlight-theme-select').forEach((picker) => {
    					const select = picker.querySelector('select');
    					if (select) select.value = theme;
    					/** @type {HTMLTemplateElement | null} */
    					const tmpl = document.querySelector(`#theme-icons`);
    					const newIcon = tmpl && tmpl.content.querySelector('.' + theme);
    					if (newIcon) {
    						const oldIcon = picker.querySelector('svg.label-icon');
    						if (oldIcon) {
    							oldIcon.replaceChildren(...newIcon.cloneNode(true).childNodes);
    						}
    					}
    				});
    			},
    		};
    	})();
    </script><template id="theme-icons"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="light astro-c6vsoqas" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" style="--sl-icon-size: 1em;"><path d="M5 class="astro-bguv2lll" lang="en" dir="ltr">    <div class="content-panel astro-7nkwcw3z"> <div class="sl-container astro-7nkwcw3z"> <h1 id="_top" class="astro-j6tvhyss">Playback &amp; Sources</h1> </div> </div> <div class="content-panel astro-7nkwcw3z"> <div class="sl-container astro-7nkwcw3z"> <div class="sl-markdown-content"> <p>Playify supports a vast array of sources and advanced playback features.</p>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="supported-sources">Supported Sources</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#supported-sources"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Supported Sources”</span></a></div>
    <p>When you use <code dir="auto">/play</code>, you can provide a direct URL or simply type a search query. Playify supports:</p>
    <ul>
    <li><strong>YouTube</strong> &#x26; <strong>YouTube Music</strong></li>
    <li><strong>SoundCloud</strong></li>
    <li><strong>Spotify</strong> (Tracks, Playlists, Albums, Release Radar)</li>
    <li><strong>Twitch</strong></li>
    <li><strong>Apple Music</strong>, <strong>Tidal</strong>, <strong>Deezer</strong>, <strong>Amazon Music</strong></li>
    <li><strong>Direct Audio Links</strong> (e.g., a <code dir="auto">.mp3</code> or <code dir="auto">.flac</code> URL)</li>
    </ul>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h3"><h3 id="local-files">Local Files</h3><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#local-files"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Local Files”</span></a></div>
    <p>You can play local files directly in Discord by using the <code dir="auto">/play-files</code> command and uploading an audio or video file directly as an attachment.</p>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="autoplay-and-stations">Autoplay and Stations</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#autoplay-and-stations"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Autoplay and Stations”</span></a></div>
    <p>Never let the music stop!</p>
    <ul>
    <li><strong>YouTube Mix:</strong> Playify will automatically fetch similar tracks related to the last played YouTube song when the queue is empty.</li>
    <li><strong>SoundCloud Stations:</strong> If you play a SoundCloud track, Autoplay will leverage SoundCloud Stations to find related tracks indefinitely.</li>
    <li>Use <code dir="auto">/autoplay</code> to toggle this behavior on or off.</li>
    </ul>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="audio-filters">Audio Filters</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#audio-filters"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Audio Filters”</span></a></div>
    <p>Modify the currently playing track in real-time with <code dir="auto">/filter</code>. Some available filters include:</p>
    <ul>
    <li>Nightcore</li>
    <li>Bass Boost</li>
    <li>Slowed &#x26; Reverb</li>
    <li>8D Audio</li>
    <li>Vaporwave</li>
    </ul>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="spotify-support">Spotify Support</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#spotify-support"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Spotify Support”</span></a></div>
    <p>Playify integrates tightly with Spotify.
    Because Spotify doesn’t provide the audio directly, Playify matches Spotify tracks against YouTube/SoundCloud equivalents.
    It supports fetching private and public playlists using <code dir="auto">SpotifyScraper</code>, entirely bypassing normal API limits.</p> </div> <footer class="sl-flex astro-3yyafb3n"> <div class="meta sl-flex astro-3yyafb3n">   </div> <div class="pagination-links print:hidden astro-u2l5gyhi" dir="ltr"> <a href="/usage/commands/" rel="prev" class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> <svg aria-hidden="true" class="astro-u2l5gyhi astro-c6vsoqas" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" style="--sl-icon-size: 1.5rem;"><path d="M17 11H9.41l3.3-3.29a1.004 1.004 0 1 0-1.42-1.42l-5 5a1 1 0 0 0-.21.33 1 1 0 0 0 0 .76 1 1 0 0 0 .21.33l5 5a1.002 1.002 0 0 0 1.639-.325 1 1 0 0 0-.219-1.095L9.41 13H17a1 1 0 0 0 0-2Z"/></svg> <span class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> Previous <br class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> <span class="link-title astro-u2l5gyhi">Commands Reference</span> </span> </a> <a href="/usage/tui-dashboard/" rel="next" class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> <svg aria-hidden="true" class="astro-u2l5gyhi astro-c6vsoqas" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" style="--sl-icon-size: 1.5rem;"><path d="M17.92 11.62a1.001 1.001 0 0 0-.21-.33l-5-5a1.003 1.003 0 1 0-1.42 1.42l3.3 3.29H7a1 1 0 0 0 0 2h7.59l-3.3 3.29a1.002 1.002 0 0 0 .325 1.639 1 1 0 0 0 1.095-.219l5-5a1 1 0 0 0 .21-.33 1 1 0 0 0 0-.76Z"/></svg> <span class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> Next <br class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> <span class="link-title astro-u2l5gyhi">TUI Dashboard</span> </span> </a> </div>  </footer> </div> </div>  </main> </div> </div> </div> </div> </body></html>

astro-67yu43on">  <main data-pagefind-body class="astro-bguv2lll" lang="en" dir="ltr">    <div class="content-panel astro-7nkwcw3z"> <div class="sl-container astro-7nkwcw3z"> <h1 id="_top" class="astro-j6tvhyss">TUI Dashboard</h1> </div> </div> <div class="content-panel astro-7nkwcw3z"> <div class="sl-container astro-7nkwcw3z"> <div class="sl-markdown-content"> <p>Playify V2 introduces a rich, interactive <strong>TUI (Terminal User Interface) Dashboard</strong> built with Python’s Rich library.</p>
    <p>When you run <code dir="auto">start.bat</code> or <code dir="auto">start.sh</code>, the dashboard automatically launches in your terminal.</p>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="whats-on-the-dashboard">What’s on the Dashboard?</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#whats-on-the-dashboard"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “What’s on the Dashboard?”</span></a></div>
    <ul>
    <li><strong>Real-time Metrics:</strong> Monitor the bot’s CPU and Memory usage.</li>
    <li><strong>Active Players:</strong> See how many servers the bot is currently playing music in.</li>
    <li><strong>Queue Info:</strong> Displays the current track and queue length.</li>
    <li><strong>Live Logs:</strong> A live, color-coded stream of the bot’s internal logs, warnings, and errors.</li>
    </ul>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="settings-menu">Settings Menu</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#settings-menu"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Settings Menu”</span></a></div>
    <p>You don’t need to manually edit config files anymore! Press <code dir="auto">S</code> while in the dashboard to open the <strong>Settings Menu</strong>.</p>
    <p>From the settings menu, you can configure:</p>
    <ul>
    <li><strong>Discord Presence:</strong> Change the bot’s status (Playing, Listening, Watching) and activity text.</li>
    <li><strong>Default Volume:</strong> Set the default starting volume for the bot when it joins a channel.</li>
    <li><strong>UI Customization:</strong> Toggle the aesthetic style of the bot’s embed messages on Discord.</li>
    </ul>
    <div class="sl-heading-wrapper level-h2"><h2 id="built-in-updater">Built-in Updater</h2><a class="sl-anchor-link" href="#built-in-updater"><span aria-hidden="true" class="sl-anchor-icon"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="currentcolor" d="m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z"></path></svg></span><span class="sr-only" data-pagefind-ignore="">Section titled “Built-in Updater”</span></a></div>
    <p>Playify includes a built-in auto-updater. You can check for updates directly from the dashboard and apply them seamlessly without needing to use <code dir="auto">git pull</code> or manual downloads.</p> </div> <footer class="sl-flex astro-3yyafb3n"> <div class="meta sl-flex astro-3yyafb3n">   </div> <div class="pagination-links print:hidden astro-u2l5gyhi" dir="ltr"> <a href="/usage/playback-and-sources/" rel="prev" class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> <svg aria-hidden="true" class="astro-u2l5gyhi astro-c6vsoqas" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" style="--sl-icon-size: 1.5rem;"><path d="M17 11H9.41l3.3-3.29a1.004 1.004 0 1 0-1.42-1.42l-5 5a1 1 0 0 0-.21.33 1 1 0 0 0 0 .76 1 1 0 0 0 .21.33l5 5a1.002 1.002 0 0 0 1.639-.325 1 1 0 0 0-.219-1.095L9.41 13H17a1 1 0 0 0 0-2Z"/></svg> <span class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> Previous <br class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> <span class="link-title astro-u2l5gyhi">Playback &amp; Sources</span> </span> </a> <a href="/troubleshooting/faq/" rel="next" class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> <svg aria-hidden="true" class="astro-u2l5gyhi astro-c6vsoqas" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" style="--sl-icon-size: 1.5rem;"><path d="M17.92 11.62a1.001 1.001 0 0 0-.21-.33l-5-5a1.003 1.003 0 1 0-1.42 1.42l3.3 3.29H7a1 1 0 0 0 0 2h7.59l-3.3 3.29a1.002 1.002 0 0 0 .325 1.639 1 1 0 0 0 1.095-.219l5-5a1 1 0 0 0 .21-.33 1 1 0 0 0 0-.76Z"/></svg> <span class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> Next <br class="astro-u2l5gyhi"> <span class="link-title astro-u2l5gyhi">FAQ</span> </span> </a> </div>  </footer> </div> </div>  </main> </div> </div> </div> </div> </body></html>

    	window.StarlightThemeProvider = (() => {
    		const storedTheme =
    			typeof localStorage !== 'undefined' && localStorage.getItem('starlight-theme');
    		const theme =
    			storedTheme ||
    			(window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: light)').matches ? 'light' : 'dark');
    		document.documentElement.dataset.theme = theme === 'light' ? 'light' : 'dark';
    		return {
    			updatePickers(theme = storedTheme || 'auto') {
    				document.querySelectorAll('starlight-theme-select').forEach((picker) => {
    					const select = picker.querySelector('select');
    					if (select) select.value = theme;
    					/** @type {HTMLTemplateElement | null} */
    					const tmpl = document.querySelector(`#theme-icons`);
    					const newIcon = tmpl && tmpl.content.querySelector('.' + theme);
    					if (newIcon) {
    						const oldIcon = picker.querySelector('svg.label-icon');
    						if (oldIcon) {
    							oldIcon.replaceChildren(...newIcon.cloneNode(true).childNodes);
    						}
    					}
    				});
    			},
    		};
    	})();

FICHIER : src\content\docs\getting-started\installation.md
================================================================================
    ---
    title: Installation
    description: How to install and run Playify on Windows, Linux, or Docker.
    ---
    
    Playify provides seamless installation scripts to get you up and running as quickly as possible.
    
    ## Windows (Recommended)
    
    1. Download the repository as a ZIP from the [GitHub releases](https://github.com/alan7383/playify) or clone it via git.
       
       ![Download ZIP](../../../assets/download-zip.png)
    
    2. Extract the ZIP file anywhere on your computer (make sure it's extracted, do not run from within the ZIP).
    3. Double-click `start.bat`.
    4. The Playify installer will automatically install Python, download FFmpeg, and prompt you for your Discord Token and Spotify keys.
    5. The TUI Dashboard will launch automatically!
    
    ## Linux
    
    Playify natively supports Linux with an automated setup script.
    
    1. Clone the repository: 
    ```bash
    git clone https://github.com/alan7383/playify.git
    ```
    2. Enter the directory: 
    ```bash
    cd playify
    ```
    3. Run the bootstrapper: 
    ```bash
    bash start.sh
    ```
    4. The script will set up your virtual environment, automatically download a local copy of FFmpeg, and launch the Dashboard.
    
    ## Docker
    
    If you prefer using Docker:
    
    1. Clone the repository:
    ```bash
    git clone https://github.com/alan7383/playify.git
    cd playify
    cp .env.example .env
    ```
    2. Edit `.env` and fill in your tokens.
    3. Start the bot:
    ```bash
    docker compose up -d --build
    ```

FICHIER : src\content\docs\getting-started\introduction.md
================================================================================
    ---
    title: Introduction
    description: Overview of Playify.
    ---
    
    # Playify
    
    **Playify** is an open-source Discord music bot built for simplicity. No web UI, no paywalls, no account required — just slash commands and music.
    
    Playify has been completely rewritten in V2 to provide a seamless, robust, and beautiful experience directly from your terminal.
    
    ## Key Features
    
    * **Interactive TUI dashboard**: Monitor resources, queue length, active players, and logs in real-time through a beautiful ASCII interface.
    * **Built-in auto-updater**: Keep your bot up to date directly from the dashboard. No `git pull` or manual downloads required.
    * **One-click installer**: Run the setup script and let Playify automatically install Python, download FFmpeg, and set up your `.env` configuration.
    * **In-app settings menu**: Configure your bot's Discord presence, default volumes, and UI customization without touching a text file.
    
    ## Sources & Playback
    
    * Play from **10+ sources**: YouTube, SoundCloud, Twitch, Spotify, Apple Music, etc.
    * **Direct audio links**: stream any public MP3, FLAC, WAV, or audio URL.
    * **Local file playback**: upload and play your own audio/video files directly.
    * **Autoplay** of similar tracks via YouTube Mix and SoundCloud Stations.
    * **Loop** and **shuffle** queue controls.
    * Audio **filters**: slowed, reverb, bass boost, nightcore, and more.
    
    ## Extras
    
    * **Lyrics** fetching and display for the current track.
    * **Karaoke mode** with synced lyrics.
    * **24/7 mode** to keep the bot in a channel permanently.
    * **Kawaii Mode** — toggle cute kaomoji responses with `/kaomoji`.
    * **Interactive queue pages**, track removal menus, and a seek interface.

FICHIER : src\content\docs\getting-started\inviting-the-bot.md
================================================================================
    ---
    title: Inviting the Bot
    description: How to add Playify to your Discord Server.
    ---
    
    Once you have your bot running (or if you are setting up the bot application for the first time), you need to invite the bot to your Discord server! It does not join automatically.
    
    Follow these steps to generate an invite link for your bot.
    
    ## 1. Go to the Developer Portal
    
    Go to the [Discord Developer Portal](https://discord.com/developers/applications) and select your application. If you don't have one yet, you must create one by clicking **New Application**.
    
    ![New Application](../../../assets/new-application.png)
    
    ## 2. Open the URL Generator
    
    In the sidebar on the left, click on **OAuth2**, and then select **URL Generator**.
    
    ![OAuth2 Menu](../../../assets/oauth2.png)
    
    ## 3. Select Scopes and Permissions
    
    To ensure Playify functions correctly and can register its slash commands, you must select the correct scopes and permissions.
    
    ### Scopes
    Check the following boxes:
    - `bot`
    - `applications.commands`
    
    ### Bot Permissions
    Once you check `bot`, a list of permissions will appear below. Check the following:
    - `View Channels`
    - `Send Messages`
    - `Embed Links`
    - `Read Message History`
    - `Connect`
    - `Speak`
    
    *(Alternatively, if you trust your own bot and don't want to deal with specific permissions, you can simply check `Administrator`.)*
    
    ## 4. Generate and Open the URL
    
    At the bottom of the page, a Generated URL will appear. Copy this URL and open it in a new tab in your web browser.
    
    ![Generated URL](../../../assets/generated-url.png)
    
    ## 5. Invite to your Server
    
    Select the server you want to add Playify to, and confirm. 
    
    Once it's in, join a Voice Channel and use `/play` to start listening!

FICHIER : src\content\docs\troubleshooting\faq.md
================================================================================
    ---
    title: FAQ & Troubleshooting
    description: Solutions to common issues.
    ---
    
    ## The bot says "FFmpeg is not found" when trying to play music!
    
    Playify normally downloads FFmpeg automatically. If it failed:
    1. You can manually download `ffmpeg.exe` and place it in the `bin/` folder inside your Playify directory (create the `bin` folder if it doesn't exist).
    2. [Download FFmpeg 6.1.1 here](https://www.videohelp.com/download/ffmpeg-6.1.1-full_build.7z?r=zndlFgBq) (extract and grab `ffmpeg.exe` from the `bin` folder).
    
    ## Do I need to enter my tokens every time?
    
    Nope! The setup script saves your tokens in a `.env` file. The next time you want to start the bot, just double-click `start.bat` (or run `start.sh`). It will instantly start the bot without asking for tokens again.
    
    ## Spotify errors or tracks not loading
    
    Check your `SPOTIFY_CLIENT_ID` and `SPOTIFY_CLIENT_SECRET` in your `.env` file. You can get these by creating an app in the [Spotify Developer Dashboard](https://developer.spotify.com/dashboard/).
    
    ## Bot is offline or unresponsive
    
    - Verify your `DISCORD_TOKEN` in the `.env` file.
    - Ensure you have invited the bot with the correct scopes and permissions (`bot`, `applications.commands`). See the [Inviting the Bot](/getting-started/inviting-the-bot) guide for details.

FICHIER : src\content\docs\usage\commands.md
================================================================================
    ---
    title: Commands Reference
    description: Exhaustive list of Playify's slash commands.
    ---
    
    Playify uses Discord's native Slash Commands. Type `/` in your server to see the full list of available commands.
    
    ## Playback
    
    | Command | Description |
    | :--- | :--- |
    | `/play <url/query>` | Play a link or search for a song. |
    | `/search <query>` | Search and choose from the top results. |
    | `/play-files <file(s)>` | Plays one or more uploaded audio or video files. |
    | `/playnext <query/file>` | Add a song or a local file to play next. |
    | `/previous` | Plays the previous song in the history. |
    
    ## Controls
    
    | Command | Description |
    | :--- | :--- |
    | `/pause` | Pause the current playback. |
    | `/resume` | Resume the playback. |
    | `/skip` | Skip the current track. |
    | `/stop` | Stop playback and disconnect the bot. |
    | `/seek` | Interactive seek, fast-forward, or rewind menu. |
    | `/jumpto` | Opens a menu to jump to a specific song in the queue. |
    | `/volume` | Adjusts the music volume for everyone (0-200%). |
    | `/reconnect` | Refresh the voice connection without losing your place. |
    
    ## Queue & Info
    
    | Command | Description |
    | :--- | :--- |
    | `/nowplaying` | Show the current song playing. |
    | `/queue` | Show the current song queue and status with pages. |
    | `/remove` | Open a menu to remove tracks from the queue. |
    | `/shuffle` | Shuffle the current queue. |
    | `/clearqueue` | Clear the current queue. |
    | `/loop` | Enable/disable looping. |
    
    ## Features & Modes
    
    | Command | Description |
    | :--- | :--- |
    | `/autoplay` | Enable/disable autoplay of similar songs. |
    | `/24_7 <mode>` | Enable or disable 24/7 mode (`normal`, `auto`, `off`). |
    | `/filter` | Applies or removes audio filters in real time. |
    | `/lyrics` | Get song lyrics from Genius. |
    | `/karaoke` | Start a synced karaoke-style lyrics display. |
    
    ## Admin & Setup
    
    | Command | Description |
    | :--- | :--- |
    | `/setup controller` | Sets or updates the channel for the persistent music controller. `(ADMIN)` |
    | `/setup allowlist` | Restricts bot commands to specific channels. `(ADMIN)` |
    | `/kaomoji` | Enable/disable kawaii mode. `(ADMIN)` |
    
    ## Misc
    
    | Command | Description |
    | :--- | :--- |
    | `/status` | Displays the bot's system status and metrics. |
    | `/support` | Shows ways to support the creator of Playify. |

FICHIER : src\content\docs\usage\playback-and-sources.md
================================================================================
    ---
    title: Playback & Sources
    description: How to play music from different platforms, use playlists, and SoundCloud stations.
    ---
    
    Playify supports a vast array of sources and advanced playback features.
    
    ## Supported Sources
    
    When you use `/play`, you can provide a direct URL or simply type a search query. Playify supports:
    
    - **YouTube** & **YouTube Music**
    - **SoundCloud**
    - **Spotify** (Tracks, Playlists, Albums, Release Radar)
    - **Twitch**
    - **Apple Music**, **Tidal**, **Deezer**, **Amazon Music**
    - **Direct Audio Links** (e.g., a `.mp3` or `.flac` URL)
    
    ### Local Files
    
    You can play local files directly in Discord by using the `/play-files` command and uploading an audio or video file directly as an attachment. 
    
    ## Autoplay and Stations
    
    Never let the music stop!
    
    - **YouTube Mix:** Playify will automatically fetch similar tracks related to the last played YouTube song when the queue is empty.
    - **SoundCloud Stations:** If you play a SoundCloud track, Autoplay will leverage SoundCloud Stations to find related tracks indefinitely.
    - Use `/autoplay` to toggle this behavior on or off.
    
    ## Audio Filters
    
    Modify the currently playing track in real-time with `/filter`. Some available filters include:
    - Nightcore
    - Bass Boost
    - Slowed & Reverb
    - 8D Audio
    - Vaporwave
    
    ## Spotify Support
    
    Playify integrates tightly with Spotify.
    Because Spotify doesn't provide the audio directly, Playify matches Spotify tracks against YouTube/SoundCloud equivalents. 
    It supports fetching private and public playlists using `SpotifyScraper`, entirely bypassing normal API limits.
    


================================================================================
FICHIER : src\content\docs\usage\tui-dashboard.md
================================================================================
    ---
    title: TUI Dashboard
    description: How to use Playify's Terminal User Interface dashboard.
    ---
    
    Playify V2 introduces a rich, interactive **TUI (Terminal User Interface) Dashboard** built with Python's Rich library.
    
    When you run `start.bat` or `start.sh`, the dashboard automatically launches in your terminal.
    
    ## What's on the Dashboard?
    
    - **Real-time Metrics:** Monitor the bot's CPU and Memory usage.
    - **Active Players:** See how many servers the bot is currently playing music in.
    - **Queue Info:** Displays the current track and queue length.
    - **Live Logs:** A live, color-coded stream of the bot's internal logs, warnings, and errors.
    
    ## Settings Menu
    
    You don't need to manually edit config files anymore! Press `S` while in the dashboard to open the **Settings Menu**.
    
    From the settings menu, you can configure:
    - **Discord Presence:** Change the bot's status (Playing, Listening, Watching) and activity text.
    - **Default Volume:** Set the default starting volume for the bot when it joins a channel.
    - **UI Customization:** Toggle the aesthetic style of the bot's embed messages on Discord.
    
    ## Built-in Updater
    
    Playify includes a built-in auto-updater. You can check for updates directly from the dashboard and apply them seamlessly without needing to use `git pull` or manual downloads.

FICHIER : README.md
================================================================================
    # Starlight Starter Kit: Basics
    
    [![Built with Starlight](https://astro.badg.es/v2/built-with-starlight/tiny.svg)](https://starlight.astro.build)
    
    ```
    npm create astro@latest -- --template starlight
    ```
    
    > 🧑‍🚀 **Seasoned astronaut?** Delete this file. Have fun!
    
    ## 🚀 Project Structure
    
    Inside of your Astro + Starlight project, you'll see the following folders and files:
    
    ```
    .
    ├── public/
    ├── src/
    │   ├── assets/
    │   ├── content/
    │   │   └── docs/
    │   └── content.config.ts
    ├── astro.config.mjs
    ├── package.json
    └── tsconfig.json
    ```
    
    Starlight looks for `.md` or `.mdx` files in the `src/content/docs/` directory. Each file is exposed as a route based on its file name.
    
    Images can be added to `src/assets/` and embedded in Markdown with a relative link.
    
    Static assets, like favicons, can be placed in the `public/` directory.
    
    ## 🧞 Commands
    
    All commands are run from the root of the project, from a terminal:
    
    | Command                   | Action                                           |
    | :------------------------ | :----------------------------------------------- |
    | `npm install`             | Installs dependencies                            |
    | `npm run dev`             | Starts local dev server at `localhost:4321`      |
    | `npm run build`           | Build your production site to `./dist/`          |
    | `npm run preview`         | Preview your build locally, before deploying     |
    | `npm run astro ...`       | Run CLI commands like `astro add`, `astro check` |
    | `npm run astro -- --help` | Get help using the Astro CLI                     |
    
    ## 👀 Want to learn more?
    
    Check out [Starlight’s docs](https://starlight.astro.build/), read [the Astro documentation](https://docs.astro.build), or jump into the [Astro Discord server](https://astro.build/chat).
